group coordinator's state machine is implemented across multiple Java source files in the group-coordinator module. There are two distinct implementations: the classic (legacy) consumer group protocol and the modern consumer group protocol.\\n\\nClassic Consumer Group State Machine:\\nThe classic protocol uses a group-level state machine defined in group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/classic/ClassicGroupState.java (sg-evals/kafka--0753c489). The ClassicGroupState enum defines five states:\\n\\n1. EMPTY: The group has no members, lingering until offsets expire. Transitions to PREPARING_REBALANCE when a new member joins.\\n2. PREPARING_REBALANCE (Join phase): The group is awaiting members to join. Members send JoinGroup requests. Transitions to COMPLETING_REBALANCE when all expected members have joined.\\n3. COMPLETING_REBALANCE (Sync phase): The group is awaiting synchronization. The leader sends SyncGroup request with assignments. Transitions to STABLE when the sync is complete.\\n4. STABLE: The group is stable with assigned partitions. Members send heartbeats to maintain membership. Transitions back to PREPARING_REBALANCE on member failure, leave, or new join.\\n5. DEAD: Final state before cleanup.\\n\\nThe ClassicGroup class (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/classic/ClassicGroup.java) manages the group state and transitions through the transitionTo() method, which validates state transitions based on validPreviousStates.\\n\\nModern Consumer Group State Machine:\\nThe modern protocol uses a different state machine defined in group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/modern/consumer/ConsumerGroup.java (sg-evals/kafka--0753c489). The ConsumerGroupState enum defines:\\n\\n1. EMPTY: No members in the group.\\n2. ASSIGNING: Members have joined and the coordinator is computing target assignment.\\n3. RECONCILING: Members are reconciling to the target assignment (revoking and acquiring partitions).\\n4. STABLE: All members are reconciled with their assignments.\\n5. DEAD: Final cleanup state.\\n\\nThe modern protocol uses a per-member state machine (MemberState in group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/modern/MemberState.java) tracking member reconciliation progress: STABLE, UNREVOKED_PARTITIONS, UNRELEASED_PARTITIONS, and UNKNOWN.\\n\\nCoordination Logic and State Transitions:\\nThe GroupMetadataManager (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupMetadataManager.java) implements the core coordination logic:\\n\\n- classicGroupJoin(): Handles JoinGroup requests for classic groups, triggering transitions from EMPTY/STABLE to PREPARING_REBALANCE\\n- classicGroupSync(): Handles SyncGroup requests, transitioning from COMPLETING_REBALANCE to STABLE\\n- classicGroupHeartbeat(): Manages heartbeats and detects member failures\\n- consumerGroupHeartbeat(): Handles heartbeats for modern consumer groups with reconciliation logic\\n\\nThe CurrentAssignmentBuilder (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/modern/consumer/CurrentAssignmentBuilder.java) encapsulates the reconciliation engine for the modern consumer group protocol, determining necessary revocation and acquisition steps to converge members to target assignments.\\n\\nGroupCoordinatorShard and GroupCoordinator provide the request handling interfaces that delegate to GroupMetadataManager for state machine operations.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":11,"cache_creation_input_tokens":1175,"cache_read_input_tokens":92392,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":1175},"output_tokens":3,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"6394bcf4-f94b-4eb3-a655-bb294c5c5a27","uuid":"7762ac41-8e1f-4c1d-bf84-448111c70e44"}
